
##################################
ACT-R 7 Version Information:
Software              : 7.0.1930-<2015-12-21> 
AGI                   : 2.0        Module based manager for AGI windows
AUDIO                 : 4.0        A module which gives the model an auditory attentional system
BOLD                  : 3.0        A module to produce BOLD response predictions from buffer request activity.
BUFFER-HISTORY        : 1.0        Module to record buffer change history for display in the environment.
BUFFER-PARAMS         : 1.0        Module to hold and control the buffer parameters
BUFFER-TRACE          : 2.0        A module that provides a buffer based tracing mechanism.
CENTRAL-PARAMETERS    : 1.2        a module that maintains parameters used by other modules
DECLARATIVE           : 2.0        The declarative memory module stores chunks from the buffers for retrieval
DEVICE                : 2.0        The device interface for a model
ENVIRONMENT           : 3.0        A module to handle the environment connection if opened
GOAL                  : 2.0        The goal module creates new goals for the goal buffer
IMAGINAL              : 3.0        The imaginal module provides a goal style buffer with a delay and an action buffer for manipulating the imaginal chunk
MOTOR                 : 4.0        Module to provide a model with virtual hands
NAMING-MODULE         : 1.3        Provides safe and repeatable new name generation for models.
PRINTING-MODULE       : 1.1        Coordinates output of the model.
PROCEDURAL            : 4.0        The procedural module handles production definition and execution
PRODUCTION-COMPILATION: 2.0        A module that assists the primary procedural module with compiling productions
PRODUCTION-HISTORY    : 1.1        Module to record production history for display in the environment.
RANDOM-MODULE         : 1.0        Provide a good and consistent source of pseudorandom numbers for all systems
RETRIEVAL-HISTORY     : 1.1        Module to record retrieval history for display in the environment.
SPEECH                : 4.0        A module to provide a model with the ability to speak
TEMPORAL              : 2.1        The temporal module is used to estimate short time intervals
UTILITY               : 3.0        A module that computes production utilities
VISION                : 5.0        A module to provide a model with a visual attention system
